## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x008C [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[0] = Entity->Race
  1: 0x0091 [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x00B1)
  2: 0x0094 [0x66] LOAD_EXT_SCHEDULER_MAIN: Load scheduler "sha1" with entities [EventEntity, EventEntity], work=ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[1]
  3: 0x00A3 [0x53] WAIT_SCHEDULER_TASK: Wait for scheduler "sha1" with entities [EventEntity, EventEntity]
  4: 0x00B0 [0x00] END_REQSTACK()

SUBROUTINE_00B1:
  5: 0x00B1 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[1] = ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[0]
  6: 0x00B6 [0x02] IF !(ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[1] > 5*) GOTO 0x00C6
  7: 0x00BE [0x08] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[1] -= 1*
  8: 0x00C3 [0x01] GOTO 0x00CB

SUBROUTINE_00C6:
  9: 0x00C6 [0x08] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[1] -= 2*
 10: 0x00CB [0x14] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[1] *= 10*
 11: 0x00D0 [0x07] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[1] += 9*
 12: 0x00D5 [0x1B] RETURN
```
